    SELECT c0."Id", c0."CartId", c0."CreatedAt", c0."IsDeleted", c0."ProductId", c0."Quantity", c0."RowVersion", c0."UpdatedAt", p0."Id" AS "Id0", p0."CategoryId", p0."CreatedAt" AS "CreatedAt0", p0."Description", p0."ImageUrl", p0."IsDeleted" AS "IsDeleted0", p0."Name", p0."Price", p0."RowVersion" AS "RowVersion0", p0."SearchVector", p0."Slug", p0."StockQuantity", p0."Tags", p0."UpdatedAt" AS "UpdatedAt0"
    FROM "CartItems" AS c0
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT p."Id", p."CategoryId", p."CreatedAt", p."Description", p."ImageUrl", p."IsDeleted", p."Name", p."Price", p."RowVersion", p."SearchVector", p."Slug", p."StockQuantity", p."Tags", p."UpdatedAt"
        FROM "Products" AS p
        WHERE NOT (p."IsDeleted")
    ) AS p0 ON c0."ProductId" = p0."Id"
) AS s ON c1."Id" = s."CartId"
ORDER BY c1."Id", s."Id"
